[08/11/24, 16.25.18] KarimT: Important Update ‼️From Monday onwards we're launching online check-ins for all the customers. To have an understanding how it looks like and which info customer sees follow the link below. It's a test one, so feel free to populate it with names and proceed. 

https://nusapenida.one/confirm/16592533

24 hours before the departure all customers will be getting auto emails with the instructions and link to their check-in page. Booking team/MOD will also need to send w/a template (in my next message). 

At the end of online check-in customer receives a QR code and can save it as pdf file on his/her mobile device. 
- Later in the morning they will present this QR check-in to manager in Sanur or Serangan who will scan it with barcode scanner or camera on a tablet. QR leads directly to customer's Rental Order in Odoo where managers in the office can see all the booking data Deposit and Collect info. 
- If collect info is not zero, managers in the office are to collect the remaining amount by cash or EDC, and give one towel or poncho towel (for Premium) and tell in person to return safely after the trip together with snorkeling guides to the trip and point that if lost or damaged charges apply, give "welcome drink" card (for Premium).
- once done managers in the office tick "Customer Checked-in and Cleared" and fill in the fields either "Collected by EDC/Bank" or "Collected by Cash" for the amount collected.

[14/12/24, 15.19.43] KarimT: Dear Team at Day Trip Bali,
 
I hope you are well.
 
I am writing to express my dissatisfaction with the private boat rental experience I recently had with your company. Unfortunately, the service and quality fell far short of the experience your advertisements promised, and I am compelled to address several issues that marred the day.
 
Firstly, the breakfast platters provided were of very poor quality. The croissants, in particular, were stale to the point of being inedible, as if they were a week old. This was disappointing and far from the fresh, high-quality catering one would expect from a service that we paid 190 000 IDR per platter for. Furthermore, despite my repeated requests for the breakfast platters to be cleared away after consumption, they were left lying around and even placed back on our table, which was unacceptable.
 
Secondly, the crew’s attire was highly unprofessional. Most of the crew were dressed in old looking and ill-fitting clothes, which detracted from the polished experience I anticipated. For a service costing 17 000 000 IDR, I expected professionalism in appearance as well as conduct.
 
Additionally, the overall condition of the boat was unsightly and unkempt. Crew belongings were scattered throughout the vessel, creating unnecessary clutter, when I asked and it was confirmed to me the boat would have a clean look. The upstairs cushions, which I specifically requested to match the photos I provided and was assured would be the same, were different and in poor condition, with visible holes and wear. The entire boat appeared run-down and far from the pictures that were provided to me before this experience.
 
That being said, I would like to acknowledge our guide, Mickey, who was very friendly and helpful. He genuinely tried his best to make our day special, and his efforts were greatly appreciated. However, the many other issues overshadowed his hard work.
 
Given the significant shortcomings, I am requesting a 30% refund of the total amount paid. Additionally, I believe the cost of the breakfast platters should be fully refunded, given their unacceptable quality. I trust that you will take these concerns seriously and address them promptly.
 
Please let me know how you intend to resolve this matter.
 
Sincerely,
Ingrid

[09/09/25, 09.41.16] Ega Accounting: Halo serangan team and kak  @⁨Widya GM Serangan Shanti⁩, just a few tips from my experience as a gelato server:


1. After scooping gelato from the center, mix and stir it again to prevent it from looking messy.
2. Keep the gelato pan tidy to minimize melting and mess around the edges.
3. Clean the showcase and glass regularly, ideally daily, to prevent fogging and odors. Make sure to turn off the showcase and let it thaw before cleaning.
4. When arranging gelato flavors in the showcase, avoid placing similar colors next to each other. Opt for contrasting colors instead, like not placing chocolate and caramel side by side.
5. For flavor tag placement, refer to the example.

Hope this helps🙏🏻

Just to clarify, our guides do share tips with the whole team(including pro photographers from vendors), this was agreed during the last meeting with the boat department, and it has been practiced ever since. The main issue isn’t the tip split, it’s the level of participation. Our guides receive most of the tips because they’re the ones actively assisting guests from start to finish: briefing, safety, photos, snorkeling assistance, etc. Meanwhile, in many cases AR55 crew are present but not proactive in helping.

We’re open to equal tip-sharing if their crew also contributes equally. Happy to align, but it needs to be based on effort, not just being on board. Let’s make sure both teams are clear on expectations going forward 🙏

We offer *Complimentary Shuttle Service* for all our Shared and Premium Shared boat tours. Our shuttle follows a convenient route with designated pick-up points available in:
- Canggu / Berawa
- Batu Belig
- Seminyak
- Legian / Kuta
- Serangan (Final Arrival)

*How it works* : Once your booking is confirmed, our manager will reach out to provide your specific nearest pick-up location, exact timing, and a detailed itinerary.

*Looking for more comfort?* If you prefer a more direct route or a later start, you are welcome to book our Private Transfer service. This is the perfect option to save time and enjoy a door-to-door experience tailored specifically to your schedule.
